<date>1561981774600< /date><text>It's a biblically sound Christian Church like any other one I've been to, and I've been to several. I have to post five stars in that this church not only has the standard extra Sunday school rooms and Nursery, but I know they monitor the nursery staff at a minimum to make sure that more than one person is there at all times. And also the person has to have a good reference before they're allowed to volunteer there. Plus like most churches don't have, certainly at the below mega-church size, they have a Welcome Center and a full coffee shop.  One time when I was having a struggle with being fully conscious and alert, I discovered I left my wallet at home and had to search for my wife to borrow some money. Turned out she was at the end of the coffee counter. And after placing my order and getting my great cup of coffee, the cashier said that's okay, it's at no charge. This one is on me. Honestly, I was moved to almost tears.

Almost forgot. They also have a video camera that recordes the entire church service, not just the sermon. And they both stream it live and recorded on DVDs. So if you can't physically attend the church, you can use any smartphone or computer and watch it live. And you can get a service from a time in the past. Personally I think that's a great value! Singing is a big part of worship, and that's what the coming together of the Saints / believers a. k. a.  church service, is all about. It's for the worshipping God, building each other up in the faith, and supporting each other. And since the recording the entire service, you can also catch the current events and whatever else is shared from the pulpit. When you're a member of a church, you want to stay connected and involved with what is going on. And also to have all the sermons available ( I don't remember how long they keep them for. I'm pretty sure it's at least 3 months.)  Is a blessing because lots of churches do things in a series. Whether it be a topic or a going through the Bible in a sequence. Show a few have to miss one of the services and don't catch the sermon, this gives you another chance to get it.
They have a real love for the people and it shows. I've been to several different Protestant churches during my 30 + years as a Christian. And this church not only does the traditional church services, but they actually make a presence outside their church grounds. At a minimum, every year they attend the cities big annual flower festival parade. And several different volunteers from their Church well walk along the edge of the Parade route and hand out free bottles of filtered water. I know they also shut down the street that their next two, and put on a Halloween festival every year. It's a place that is well-lit, of course the only friendly, lots of free activities for the kids including face painting and making crafts. They have a jumping castle. It's something that my family has been attending for several years and we hadn't attended that church. But that was its main goal. To provide a safe and fun place for all the kids and trick-or-treaters to go to. And at that they excelled!<//text><pictures>None<//pictures><rating>5<//rating>< name>
Mr. Ed</name>

I love our church and its impact on people inside and outside our walls. We are welcoming to all and have the honor of having many active duty military as a part of our congregation. Children and youth are a high priority to us as is their safety. We offer small groups and various classes to help people grow. We have a place for everyone to use their gifts and talents as we Do Church as a Team. For those dealing with various difficulties of life, we offer Life Support and also Person 2 Person support for those who attend. f I was not the pastor here, I would attend here - some of the best people in the region right here at LFC. Thanks for reading my review.<//Text>

In fact, everyone in the store seemed to know kne another (or at least the guy behind the counter) and it almost seemed like a social club...I kinda felt like the odd man out but I held back my tears ubtil I left the store and had a good cry in  my car outside...I was teased as a child and this brought it all back so if you have been through similar traumas as a child I would not recommend this place.

Just to be clean that last part was a joke, I actually found the familiar, friendly atmosphere pretty cool ðŸ¥³<//Text>

< review>
Great little cigar lounge tucked away in the small town of Visalia.  Its one of the few things I look forward to when out in this part of town.

Selection:  Selection is pretty decent here. The last time i was in there was an Kristoff event and the owner made me feel at home.

Pricing is on point.  Little on the high side, but its the CA tax, nothing major here.

Crew that hangs here is very friendly, even had a conversation on religion with a guy (i am not religious.

My one grip is they close  too early.   I get out of work around 5, change and head over.  I am usually not finished with my first smoke by closing time.  The owner is really cool and will let you finish but keep this bad boy open another couple hours and profit.

Nice lounge to get some work done in. Also BYOB which is really nice.</review>

< Text>
We were here celebrating our 10 years dating anniversary. Very friendly staff, great service for sure. But the taste of food does not match the price unfortunately. We ordered the special salmon belly bread, and butternut squash soup, the lamb. For the price point I would expect above average food experience. But all of the dishes is lack of the flavor. The salmon bread is actually the best of all. The butternut squash soup cant taste the freshness and sweetness of the butternut squash, and the lambðŸ™ˆso dry and not much flavor, just a little bit of cumin taste on the bone part of the rack, I wish it would have a bit more sauce besides the circle. I cook better dry rub lamb rack at home, definitely not worth 38 something dollar. But the vegetable(mushroom, pickle) surprisingly so flavorful. My husband's waygu beef steak wasn't juicy or full of beef flavor either, his dish is 40 something dollar. I think they need to master how to bring out the meat flavor as well as keep the juice inside the meat.<//Text>

<Rate>5<//Rate>< text>
Fantastic restaurant in Solvang.  The chef has some Michelin heritage under his belt and that experience shows up in the delightful menu.  Chose from a variety of offerings to make up a good meal.

The duck wings were a spectacular start. Followed by amazing beets, Spanish octopus, and wagyu.  Did not care for the pork belly but the pear ball for desert more than made up for any other shortcomings.  It was a hard chocolate ball, once cracked open reveals nuggets of deliciousness.

Wine selection by the glass is primarily their own house wines (Coquelicot).  Had the Viognier, Pinot noir, and Grenache.  While the wines are OK I donâ€™t think that they are the best choices.   They do have other wines to chose from by the bottle and would opt for that next time.<//text>

Had a wonderful experience. I had the 2-2-1 and each course was divine. As a starter I had the Duck wings and kimchi cracklings. After eating the wings I will be hard pressed to enjoy chicken wings again. The cracklings reminded me of fried pork skin in appearance but they were light and airy and actually had no resemblance to the kimchi I have had in Korean restaurants. My two entrees were the pork cheeks with delicious mashed potatoes and the wagyu beef with roasted fingerling type potatoes. Both exceeded my expectations and my dessert was chocolate mousse with honeycomb brittle. Michael, our server, was efficient and helpful and didn't rush us through each course. It was a relaxing and thoroughly wonderful experience.<//Text>

<review>This review is long long long overdue. I don't even know where to begin...

I visited a few orthodontists who said the only way to fix my open bite was with surgery. I couldn't eat burritos or pizza without a fork and knife and I had a terrible lisp. I really wanted to fix it but was unwilling to have my face sawed. Finally, a friend referred me to Dr. Bergh, who was the only person willing to try a less invasive method to fix my bite.

< Review>
Waited incredibly long. The people at the door didn't even say wait will be more than 30 min. Nobody said we could take a seat in the seating area. They didn't offer us to sit at the bar either. When we finally got to our table we waited additional 15 minutes before our order was taken. Overall wait was 1 hour and 10 minutes. After the food finally arrived they got my eggs and my one kids eggs wrong. I asked for medium done got underdone eggs that had runny egg whites. My son was offered more orange juice, but never got it. We initially wanted hot chocolate, but the place had run out of stock. The meat I got was not nice it had too much sugar added while cooked. Onions were undercooked. The waiters and the hostess had very heavy accent and were very difficult to communicate with.
Overall, quite a bad experience.

Probably never going back at this location, despite being the closest to my house.<//Review>
